msg:Choosing Jue Le Fu Hotel was the right choice for this trip to Xi'an; meeting the hotel housekeeper Zhao Hongxia was the luckiest thing for this trip to Xi'an.

This time we came to Xi'an just after the heating period ended, and the central air conditioning was not yet turned on. The hotel was stuffy and unbearable on the first night. As newcomers to Xi'an, we didn't understand this situation at first. We thought the hotel air conditioning was broken and asked the housekeeper to repair it. The housekeeper apologized to us immediately and promised to solve it. After returning the next afternoon, Zhao Hongxia changed the room for us, arranged a cold air blower and a humidifier, and arranged a foot bath bucket and hot milk before bed for fear that we would not sleep well. Later, when the hotel's central air conditioning was turned on, the housekeeper Zhao Hongxia also informed me on WeChat as soon as possible.

As a star-rated hotel, Jue Le Fu not only has standardized services, but also can be customized, and provides considerate and meticulous services to every visiting guest. The service of housekeeper Zhao Hongxia is also warm, considerate and measured. Thank you very much! ! There is also service staff Xu Yajuan, whose service is also in place.

I hope that friends who come to Xi'an in the future will choose the Juelufu Hotel after reading this comment. If you want to find a hotel with a superior location and meticulous service, Juelufu will be your best choice!

msg:Very satisfied with the stay experience, but unfortunately the highest score can only be rated 5 points. This is the second time to stay. The subway was not repaired when I came last time. This time I revisited the old place and the experience was better than the last time.
Thanks to the housekeeper Xiao Ma, knowing that there were children staying, he equipped the children's toilet and humidifier. Hot milk, yogurt and snacks were provided every day, and the experience was full.
Thanks to the guest room sister Mu Chunling, the room was very clean, and a peeling knife was specially prepared for us to eat pears and apples. By the way, the pears are so sweet!
Two small suggestions for the hotel's reference for the next renovation.
1. It is recommended to install an independent light control in the bathroom, otherwise when the light is turned on in the morning, the bedroom light will also be on, affecting sleep.
2. The opening and closing sounds of the cabinet door and the bathroom door are a little loud, so they can be lubricated regularly.
3. It would be better if there were more sockets at the bedside.
In short, this stay is still very comfortable. Next time I come to Xi'an, I must stay at Jue Le Fu. I also sincerely recommend it to other tourists.

The hotel I stayed in was reasonably priced but had free laundry and drying services. Thirdly, the carpet in the room was not suitable for walking barefoot.
